Google’s culture is inclusive, and even as a janitor, you’re treated with respect and can enjoy some perks, like access to the company&#x27;s cafeterias. The environment is fast-paced, with a focus on efficiency and attention to detail. However, the job can be physically demanding, requiring long hours of standing and moving around.
